2834 #define __HAL_RCC_GPIOD_CLK_ENABLE() do { \
2835  __IO uint32_t tmpreg = 0x00U; \
2836  SET_BIT(RCC->AHB1ENR, RCC_AHB1ENR_GPIODEN);\
2837  /* Delay after an RCC peripheral clock enabling */ \
2838  tmpreg = READ_BIT(RCC->AHB1ENR, RCC_AHB1ENR_GPIODEN);\
2839  UNUSED(tmpreg); \
2840  } while(0)
2841 #define __HAL_RCC_GPIOE_CLK_ENABLE() do { \
2842  __IO uint32_t tmpreg = 0x00U; \
2843  SET_BIT(RCC->AHB1ENR, RCC_AHB1ENR_GPIOEEN);\
2844  /* Delay after an RCC peripheral clock enabling */ \
2845  tmpreg = READ_BIT(RCC->AHB1ENR, RCC_AHB1ENR_GPIOEEN);\
2846  UNUSED(tmpreg); \
2847  } while(0)
2848 #define __HAL_RCC_CRC_CLK_ENABLE() do { \
2849  __IO uint32_t tmpreg = 0x00U; \
2850  SET_BIT(RCC->AHB1ENR, RCC_AHB1ENR_CRCEN);\
2851  /* Delay after an RCC peripheral clock enabling */ \
2852  tmpreg = READ_BIT(RCC->AHB1ENR, RCC_AHB1ENR_CRCEN);\
2853  UNUSED(tmpreg); \
2854  } while(0)
2855 #define __HAL_RCC_BKPSRAM_CLK_ENABLE() do { \

5411 /*------------------------------- PLL Configuration --------------------------*/
5412 #if defined(STM32F410Tx) || defined(STM32F410Cx) || defined(STM32F410Rx) || defined(STM32F446xx) ||\
5413  defined(STM32F469xx) || defined(STM32F479xx) || defined(STM32F412Zx) || defined(STM32F412Vx) || \
5414  defined(STM32F412Rx) || defined(STM32F412Cx)
5448 #define __HAL_RCC_PLL_CONFIG(__RCC_PLLSource__, __PLLM__, __PLLN__, __PLLP__, __PLLQ__,__PLLR__) \
5449  (RCC->PLLCFGR = ((__RCC_PLLSource__) | (__PLLM__) | \
5450  ((__PLLN__) << POSITION_VAL(RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLN)) | \
5451  ((((__PLLP__) >> 1) -1) << POSITION_VAL(RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLP)) | \
5452  ((__PLLQ__) << POSITION_VAL(RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLQ)) | \
5453  ((__PLLR__) << POSITION_VAL(RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLR))))
5454 #else
5484 #define __HAL_RCC_PLL_CONFIG(__RCC_PLLSource__, __PLLM__, __PLLN__, __PLLP__, __PLLQ__) \
5485  (RCC->PLLCFGR = (0x20000000U | (__RCC_PLLSource__) | (__PLLM__)| \
5486  ((__PLLN__) << POSITION_VAL(RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLN)) | \
5487  ((((__PLLP__) >> 1) -1) << POSITION_VAL(RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLP)) | \
5488  ((__PLLQ__) << POSITION_VAL(RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLQ))))
5489  #endif /* STM32F410xx || STM32F446xx || STM32F469xx || STM32F479xx || STM32F412Zx || STM32F412Vx || STM32F412Rx || STM32F412Cx */
